defined_text = {
	name = GetMotherInLaw

	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { character = FROM }
			is_female = yes
		}
		localisation_key = GetRelation_MotherOfHusband
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { character = FROM }
			is_female = no
		}
		localisation_key = GetRelation_MotherOfWife
	}
	fallback_text = {
		localisation_key = GetMotherInLaw_FB
	}
}

		}
		localisation_key = String_MothersChildAdj
	}
	text = {

			#multiplayer = no

				father_even_if_dead = { any_child_even_if_dead = { character = ROOT } }
			}

#Returns the string named "ÃªÃ " for female characters, "Ã¨Ã­" for NON-ALTNAMED religion male characters (Ã­Ã Ã¯Ã°Ã¨Ã¬Ã¥Ã°, Ã¬Ã³Ã±Ã³Ã«Ã¼Ã¬Ã Ã­ÃªÃ /Ã¬Ã³Ã±Ã³Ã«Ã¼Ã¬Ã Ã­Ã¨Ã­)
defined_text = {
	name = __Ã¨Ã­ #GetKaIn_AltRel_TT_Ã¨Ã­

	text = {
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
			NOT = { FROM = { always = yes } }
			has_game_started = yes
		}
		localisation_key = END_KA
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
			NOT = { FROM = { always = yes } }
			has_game_started = yes
			is_female = no
		}
		localisation_key = END_IN
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
			OR = {
				FROM = { always = yes }
				NOT = { has_game_started = yes }
			}
		}
		localisation_key = END_IN
	}
}
